	}

	id = HYE_once_and_for_all
	icon = GFX_once_and_for_all
	cost = 7.2
	available = {
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		has_army_manpower = { size > 124999 }
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = HYE_every_hyena_a_gun
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = HYE_dig_our_heels_in
	}
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = HYE_preemptive_strike }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 500
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = THU
	will_lead_to_war_with = GYZ
	will_lead_to_war_with = STM
	will_lead_to_war_with = SLC
	relative_position_id = HYE_every_hyena_a_gun

	y = 2

					}
				} 
			}

					type = annex_everything 
					target = SLC
				}
			}

				type = annex_everything 
				target = SLC 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					}
				} 
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				create_wargoal = { 
					type = annex_everything 
					target = THU
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = { 
				type = annex_everything

		}
		if = {

				type = medium_plane_airframe_0

				amount = 30
			}
		}

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

				}
			}

				}

				}
